Change Log[¶](https://docs.blender.org/api/current/change_log.html#change-log "Link to this heading")
=====================================================================================================

Changes in Blender’s Python API between releases.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **fcurves**

*   **groups**

*   **id_root**
